<span id="freeTextContainer11511347458950339960"><blockquote>
  <b>"Dreams only come true if you point yourself in their direction."<b></b></b>
</blockquote><br/>The love story of Ryan and Taryn is great, really! Both books are full of sweet and sexy moments that warmed my heart. <br/><blockquote>
<br/> "We were the only two people in the world.<br/> Sitting in the street.<br/> In a small stream.<br/> In the rain.<br/> And just like that, my gorgeous man replaced bad with another slice of great."<br/><br/><div><a href='http://pinterest.com/pin/241787073715523473/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><span>[image error]</span></a></div>
<div></div>
<br/>
</blockquote><br/>I absolutely loved the characters, especially my sweet and down-to-earth Ryan. As my friend Amaia told me, he is the o</span>
  <span id="freeText11511347458950339960" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>"Dreams only come true if you point yourself in their direction."<b></b></b>
</blockquote><br>The love story of Ryan and Taryn is great, really! Both books are full of sweet and sexy moments that warmed my heart. <br><blockquote>
<br> "We were the only two people in the world.<br> Sitting in the street.<br> In a small stream.<br> In the rain.<br> And just like that, my gorgeous man replaced bad with another slice of great."<br><br><div><a href="http://pinterest.com/pin/241787073715523473/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><span>[image error]</span></a></div>
<div></div>
<br>
</blockquote><br>I absolutely loved the characters, especially my sweet and down-to-earth Ryan. As my friend Amaia told me, he is the one who makes the story worth reading and I agree with her.<br><blockquote>"You are home for me. You'll always be my home, Taryn"<br><br>"Tar, I knew that very first day I stumbled into your pub that you were the one. I think I fell in love with you when you were rubbing that shit on my cuts."</blockquote><br>Despite of the lack of drama and angst in this last book I enjoyed it but I must confess that I liked <i>"Love Unscripted"</i> more than this one. <br>In <i>"Love Unrehearsed"</i>, Ryan and Taryn had to deal with the celebrities' lifestyle, a world full of evil people who tried to ruin their life together over and over again.<br><blockquote>"How can our love for each other possibly survive through all these constant bombardments, accusations, and heartaches?"<br><br><div><a href="http://pinterest.com/pin/241787073714916762/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><span>[image error]</span></a></div>
<div></div>
<br>
</blockquote>But what they got was the opposite of what they wanted. I really loved to see how they finally get over their trust issues, build a life together and also how their relationship got stronger and unbreakable.<br><blockquote>"I wrote that song on the airplane. I wanted you to know how serious I am about us. How much I want you in my life, Taryn. I meant it when I said forever. That's why. You are it for me. But the me that knelt in front of you that night and the me that is standing in front of you right now is not the same me that's our there in the spotlight. They only get the outside, not the inside. That's four you".</blockquote><br>I wanted to read about fame and the celebrity world and in that subject the storyline doesn't disappoint. But I've to complain about the senseless at some parts of the book. <br>The story as a whole is so long and sometimes it gets kind of boring but as I said before it's worth making the effort to read it. <br><blockquote>"As soon as I saw him there with his hands clasped in front of him, his hair gently tussled by the ocean breeze, that breathtaking smile he wore just for me -nothing else mattered. This man was my everything."<br><br>"You always twine our fingers together when you make love to me."<br><br><div><a href="http://pinterest.com/pin/241787073715642606/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><span>[image error]</span></a></div>
<div></div>
<br>
</blockquote>Gonna miss you Ryan! <br><br><div>

<div id="review_372037616" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/372037616" />
    <a title="Kelly &#39;Perusing Princesses blog&#39;" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9535769-kelly-perusing-princesses-blog"><img alt="Kelly &#39;Perusing Princesses blog&#39;" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393856771p2/9535769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/372037616?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelly &#39;Perusing Princesses blog&#39;" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelly &#39;Perusing Princesses blog&#39;" href="/user/show/9535769-kelly-perusing-princesses-blog">Kelly &#39;Perusing Princesses blog&#39;</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9535769-kelly-perusing-princesses-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9535769-kelly-perusing-princesses-blog?shelf=awe-inspiring">awe-inspiring</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer372037616" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15032039291161508685">Book Review: Love Unrehearsed – Tina Reber - 5*<br/><br/>I waited a few hours before writing this review, simply because after I finished it, I had to take a deep breath to regulate my heartbeat and hug my kindle to my chest while a huge happy smile exploded across my face. It was also a little bittersweet, because I had come to the end of an incredible journey, with two of my favourite characters, the lovely Ryan and Taryn.<br/><br/>The most beautiful thing about this book was playing witness to the growth of each</span>
  <span id="freeText15032039291161508685" style="display:none">Book Review: Love Unrehearsed – Tina Reber - 5*<br /><br />I waited a few hours before writing this review, simply because after I finished it, I had to take a deep breath to regulate my heartbeat and hug my kindle to my chest while a huge happy smile exploded across my face. It was also a little bittersweet, because I had come to the end of an incredible journey, with two of my favourite characters, the lovely Ryan and Taryn.<br /><br />The most beautiful thing about this book was playing witness to the growth of each character. They had come a long way as the ultimate sacrifice of Ryan’s fame was already paid towards the end of Love Unscripted, and this sequel, Love Unrehearsed plays testament to how true love really can conquer all. The love and support that Ryan and Taryn both hold for each-other is almost heroic and what made this book a truly exceptional read. Yes, there are a few knocks and bumps along the way – well okay, a little more than a few, but each scenario that played out was met with maturity and an understanding that helped to make their relationship foundations even stronger.<br /><br />Love Unrehearsed starts off pretty much a week or so where Unscripted left off. Taryn is now a firm fixture within Ryan’s entourage but her presence is still met with trepidation and new fears develop with regards to their engagement between Ryan’s managers and press agents. Close friends and family are the only support system Ryan and Taryn can believe in, but things become difficult when Taryn is met with the dilemma that she is slowly becoming a celebrity herself. Being engaged to the most eligible A-Star Hollywood actor will always have its consequences. Crazed fans, paparazzi, stalkers and a hidden family secret throws Taryn back into the depths of drama 101 but the only difference this time is that Ryan isn’t taking any chances. He loves Taryn and by making her his total number one priority could prove potentially dangerous and destroy everything he has worked for…<br /><br />Follow Ryan and Taryn as they embark on their next chapter, and revel in the magic of how a small town girl captured the heart of a boy the day he ran into her pub. The boy, who just so happens to make movies for a living.<br /><br />Watch out for the epilogue, it’s pure swoonworthy beauty. An Incredible story that is wonderfully written and makes you fall in love all over again, with words. Tina Reber, you are undoubtedly one very talented lady, and I am so pleased that I found you.<br /><br />5 Mega Epic Worthy Swoony Stars. *****<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15032039291161508685" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer408048810" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13454345745028438438">There are literally no words to describe how much I love this 2-book series and how much Ryan, Taryn and all the other characters have completely captured my heart not once, but twice. I commend Tina Reber for writing this amazing book and giving me something I will never forget.<br/><br/>After finishing book 1, I thought there was no way I could ever love the second one more but OH MY GOD was I wrong. Ryan Christensen says the most steamiest, sweetest and total drool-worthy things and he will definitely </span>
  <span id="freeText13454345745028438438" style="display:none">There are literally no words to describe how much I love this 2-book series and how much Ryan, Taryn and all the other characters have completely captured my heart not once, but twice. I commend Tina Reber for writing this amazing book and giving me something I will never forget.<br /><br />After finishing book 1, I thought there was no way I could ever love the second one more but OH MY GOD was I wrong. Ryan Christensen says the most steamiest, sweetest and total drool-worthy things and he will definitely be on my book boyfriend list forever! I love how Taryn and Ryan's relationship has already developed well in this book and Tina just does such a <b>fan-freaking-tastic</b> job on selling the reader how it is in the life of dating a movie star. Everything blends so easily and you can easily picture all the drama they have to go through because of his career and I give major props to her for making this story so real for me.<br /><br />I loved all the steamy romantic scenes that happened all around the world and the bets the boys and girls would have against each other to see who would last the longest in bed had me laughing hard!<br /><br /><b>"But I think he broke my vagina."-Marie</b><br /><br />I also love that Taryn is such a strong female character, she doesn't take people's crap, doesn't need a man to support her and doesn't let stuck up jealous girls get to her. I know if I were in her shoes I would become a crazy woman after all that happens to her, but she just lets it go because she knows as long as Ryan loves her, nothing else matters.<br /><br />The epilogue at the end was very sweet and I'm so happy they finally had their happily ever after! *SQUEE* I am smiling so big right now lol I wish there was more of Taryn and Ryan's relationship to read about, but I'm very pleased with how everything ended and I can honestly say I don't think I'll ever read a more honest to god love story in my life. This book is complete perfection and it gave me everything I could ever want in a romance novel.<br /><br />&lt;3</span>
  <a data-text-id="13454345745028438438" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

For example, LU2 picks up a week after the couple became engaged at the end of LU1 and Taryn's best friend and husband are in love and happy. Suddenly in LU2 they are separating? It came out of no where and now there is something starting with her and the bodyguard. <br /><br />To be fair, I will not rate the book until I finish reading it. I may end up loving it but 50% in, I am bored and started reading other books instead. I love Love Unscripted and had such high hopes for Love Unrehearsed. Hopefully I can finish it soon and give it a real review.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16675747999989681951">It was nice to pick up the Ryan/Taryn story again, but I felt like the story was all over the place. There was so much drama, it became unbelievable. To be fair - I had very high expectations based on the first novel, so this book had the bar set very high at the outset. There was less plot and character development than the first Love installment. There were also a lot more steamy scenes this go around which I didn't care for...it made the book appear longer than it really was. Instead, I wish </span>
  <span id="freeText16675747999989681951" style="display:none">It was nice to pick up the Ryan/Taryn story again, but I felt like the story was all over the place. There was so much drama, it became unbelievable. To be fair - I had very high expectations based on the first novel, so this book had the bar set very high at the outset. There was less plot and character development than the first Love installment. There were also a lot more steamy scenes this go around which I didn't care for...it made the book appear longer than it really was. Instead, I wish some of those pages had focused more on what was going on inside the characters' heads. Don't get me wrong - the plot was there, and there is plenty of action, but I didn't feel like I learned much more about what drives the characters. Overall, I'm glad I read the sequel so the story is wrapped up, but I was hoping for something more epic. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('e4Fv0dNOOVysLKcF+sMfT1JR/YLc7h9Zrjv+7ijNKXfEF32K3eyeHftHRXW0IweYYzjLQJDPZabPOE76f8pjzA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('b4GXpEu5LMQoz25b423azepBJrT6nYV1ZE1zR8txGnLQF4X/RRuLhX+kjCutjcIa2ygQdra8/4oFTsNTnHZQyQ==')})
  }
